				<article id="post-11" class="entry content-bg single-entry post-footer-area-boxed post-11 page type-page status-publish has-post-thumbnail hentry">
	<div class="entry-content-wrap">
		<header class="entry-header page-title title-align-inherit title-tablet-align-inherit title-mobile-align-inherit">
	<h1 class="entry-title">NID Card Online Check &#8211; NID Card Check Bangladesh</h1></header><!-- .entry-header -->

<div class="entry-content single-content">
	
<p>NID Card Check (National Identity Card Check) is a crucial service used for verifying the identity of citizens. This service allows the details of an individual&#8217;s national identity card to be checked either online or offline. </p>



<p>In countries like Bangladesh, where a national identity card is mandatory for every citizen, the <strong><a href="https://nidcadonlinechecksbd.com/" data-type="link" data-id="https://nidcadonlinechecksbd.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">NID Card Online Check</a></strong> service proves extremely beneficial not only for government agencies but also for banks, educational institutions, and private companies. This service helps prevent fraud, ensure accurate identification, and provide identity verification for various services.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-966f14b034677afaec60b23e13cd2eef" style="color:#4e6c50"><strong>NID Card Online Check </strong></h2>



<p></p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-b6001bb9c79a8c3e77c9489c3eb0be96">How to Use This Tool</h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>This tool is use for very simple process. Please Follow these steps.</p>

<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_1ba52a-6e"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_check-circle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 512 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M504 256c0 136.967-111.033 248-248 248S8 392.967 8 256 119.033 8 256 8s248 111.033 248 248zM227.314 387.314l184-184c6.248-6.248 6.248-16.379 0-22.627l-22.627-22.627c-6.248-6.249-16.379-6.249-22.628 0L216 308.118l-70.059-70.059c-6.248-6.248-16.379-6.248-22.628 0l-22.627 22.627c-6.248 6.248-6.248 16.379 0 22.627l104 104c6.249 6.249 16.379 6.249 22.628.001z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Step 2:</strong> Click on &#8220;<strong>Submit</strong>&#8221; button.</span></li>

<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_0d9c1b-f6"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_check-circle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 512 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M504 256c0 136.967-111.033 248-248 248S8 392.967 8 256 119.033 8 256 8s248 111.033 248 248zM227.314 387.314l184-184c6.248-6.248 6.248-16.379 0-22.627l-22.627-22.627c-6.248-6.249-16.379-6.249-22.628 0L216 308.118l-70.059-70.059c-6.248-6.248-16.379-6.248-22.628 0l-22.627 22.627c-6.248 6.248-6.248 16.379 0 22.627l104 104c6.249 6.249 16.379 6.249 22.628.001z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Step 4:</strong> Then Again Enter your <strong>detail</strong>.</span></li>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_99dd79-26"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-b7c6a3b46a7f657b568da3c1f5961fe9">NID Card Check By Birth Certificate</h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Follow these steps to check your NID card by Birth Certificate:</span></p>



<p></p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="735" height="945" src="https://nidcardonlinechecks.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/birth-certificate-blank-format-bd.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-672" style="width:385px;height:auto" srcset="https://nidcardonlinechecks.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/birth-certificate-blank-format-bd.jpg 735w, https://nidcardonlinechecks.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/08/birth-certificate-blank-format-bd-233x300.jpg 233w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 735px) 100vw, 735px" /></figure>
</div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items11_156899-d8 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_3ba8a4-46"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Access the Online Portal: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">Go to the official website of the Bangladesh </span><a href="https://www.nidw.gov.bd/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">NID service portal</span></a></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_c3712b-41"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Navigate to the Verification Section: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">Look for the section related to NID <a href="https://policeclearancebd.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Police verification</a> or birth certificate-based checks.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_5a47b2-48"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Enter Birth Certificate Information: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">Input the required details from the birth certificate, such as the <strong>birth registration number</strong>, <strong>date of birth</strong>, and<strong> full name</strong>.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_b0d071-d9"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Provide Additional Details: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">Enter additional personal information if required, such as parents&#8217; <strong>names</strong>, place of birth, and other identifying information (optional: police clearance).</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_4b49d3-84"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Submit the Information: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">After filling in all the necessary details, submit the form.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_84bffa-bd"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Verification Process: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">The system will process the information and cross-check it with the database.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_c40ee0-c6"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Receive Verification Status: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">Once the verification is complete, you will receive the status of the <strong>NID card check</strong>. This will confirm whether the provided details match the records in the national database.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_d4a8a5-a1"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Download or Print the Verification Report: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">If required, download or print the verification report for your records.</span></span></li>
</ul></div>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-0d81ce8b281278eabedda50720ed373f"><b><strong>NID Card Check Chittagong</strong></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items11_9fc9a9-4a kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_3cf63d-ad"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Visit the official NID portal: https://services.nidw.gov.bd</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_e7d5c6-08"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Click on &#8220;Register&#8221; or log in if already registered</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_b23409-f8"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Enter your NID number/form number, date of birth, and captcha code</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_123495-c6"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">Submit and verify using the OTP sent to your registered mobile number</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_117c95-40"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text">After login, view or download your NID card in PDF format</span></li>
</ul></div>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_c911ed-8c"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-ac0019fd1bfcd8efe3e69414aa777b64"><b><strong>NID Card Check by NID Wallet App</strong></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Follow these steps to check your NID card by NID wallet app:</span></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items11_5afbb1-3a kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-7e84fdf0c8f00045ba5410c852573626"><b>NID Card Check By Mobile Number</b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Follow these steps to check your NID card by Mobile Number:</span></p>



<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items11_ce3839-0b kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_bf9fc5-8d"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-ic_circleRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 8 8"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M4 0c-2.21 0-4 1.79-4 4s1.79 4 4 4 4-1.79 4-4-1.79-4-4-4zm0 1l3 3-3 3v-2h-3v-2h3v-2z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Step 1:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> On your mobile phone, open the dialer application where you usually make phone calls.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_207268-12"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-ic_circleRight kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 8 8"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M4 0c-2.21 0-4 1.79-4 4s1.79 4 4 4 4-1.79 4-4-1.79-4-4-4zm0 1l3 3-3 3v-2h-3v-2h3v-2z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Step 2:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Enter the code </span><b>*1600#</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> into the dialer.</span></span></li>
</ul></div>

<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_5ae2dc-d4"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_hand-point-right kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 512 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M512 199.652c0 23.625-20.65 43.826-44.8 43.826h-99.851c16.34 17.048 18.346 49.766-6.299 70.944 14.288 22.829 2.147 53.017-16.45 62.315C353.574 425.878 322.654 448 272 448c-2.746 0-13.276-.203-16-.195-61.971.168-76.894-31.065-123.731-38.315C120.596 407.683 112 397.599 112 385.786V214.261l.002-.001c.011-18.366 10.607-35.889 28.464-43.845 28.886-12.994 95.413-49.038 107.534-77.323 7.797-18.194 21.384-29.084 40-29.092 34.222-.014 57.752 35.098 44.119 66.908-3.583 8.359-8.312 16.67-14.153 24.918H467.2c23.45 0 44.8 20.543 44.8 43.826zM96 200v192c0 13.255-10.745 24-24 24H24c-13.255 0-24-10.745-24-24V200c0-13.255 10.745-24 24-24h48c13.255 0 24 10.745 24 24zM68 368c0-11.046-8.954-20-20-20s-20 8.954-20 20 8.954 20 20 20 20-8.954 20-20z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Type the Message:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> In the message body, type NID followed by a space.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_ff482f-84"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_hand-point-right kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 512 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M512 199.652c0 23.625-20.65 43.826-44.8 43.826h-99.851c16.34 17.048 18.346 49.766-6.299 70.944 14.288 22.829 2.147 53.017-16.45 62.315C353.574 425.878 322.654 448 272 448c-2.746 0-13.276-.203-16-.195-61.971.168-76.894-31.065-123.731-38.315C120.596 407.683 112 397.599 112 385.786V214.261l.002-.001c.011-18.366 10.607-35.889 28.464-43.845 28.886-12.994 95.413-49.038 107.534-77.323 7.797-18.194 21.384-29.084 40-29.092 34.222-.014 57.752 35.098 44.119 66.908-3.583 8.359-8.312 16.67-14.153 24.918H467.2c23.45 0 44.8 20.543 44.8 43.826zM96 200v192c0 13.255-10.745 24-24 24H24c-13.255 0-24-10.745-24-24V200c0-13.255 10.745-24 24-24h48c13.255 0 24 10.745 24 24zM68 368c0-11.046-8.954-20-20-20s-20 8.954-20 20 8.954 20 20 20 20-8.954 20-20z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Enter Form Number:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> After the space, enter your Form Number.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_547671-40"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_hand-point-right kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 512 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M512 199.652c0 23.625-20.65 43.826-44.8 43.826h-99.851c16.34 17.048 18.346 49.766-6.299 70.944 14.288 22.829 2.147 53.017-16.45 62.315C353.574 425.878 322.654 448 272 448c-2.746 0-13.276-.203-16-.195-61.971.168-76.894-31.065-123.731-38.315C120.596 407.683 112 397.599 112 385.786V214.261l.002-.001c.011-18.366 10.607-35.889 28.464-43.845 28.886-12.994 95.413-49.038 107.534-77.323 7.797-18.194 21.384-29.084 40-29.092 34.222-.014 57.752 35.098 44.119 66.908-3.583 8.359-8.312 16.67-14.153 24.918H467.2c23.45 0 44.8 20.543 44.8 43.826zM96 200v192c0 13.255-10.745 24-24 24H24c-13.255 0-24-10.745-24-24V200c0-13.255 10.745-24 24-24h48c13.255 0 24 10.745 24 24zM68 368c0-11.046-8.954-20-20-20s-20 8.954-20 20 8.954 20 20 20 20-8.954 20-20z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Enter Date of Birth</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">: Then, add another space and enter your Date of Birth in the format <strong>DD-MM-YY</strong>.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_f96082-d0"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_hand-point-right kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 512 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M512 199.652c0 23.625-20.65 43.826-44.8 43.826h-99.851c16.34 17.048 18.346 49.766-6.299 70.944 14.288 22.829 2.147 53.017-16.45 62.315C353.574 425.878 322.654 448 272 448c-2.746 0-13.276-.203-16-.195-61.971.168-76.894-31.065-123.731-38.315C120.596 407.683 112 397.599 112 385.786V214.261l.002-.001c.011-18.366 10.607-35.889 28.464-43.845 28.886-12.994 95.413-49.038 107.534-77.323 7.797-18.194 21.384-29.084 40-29.092 34.222-.014 57.752 35.098 44.119 66.908-3.583 8.359-8.312 16.67-14.153 24.918H467.2c23.45 0 44.8 20.543 44.8 43.826zM96 200v192c0 13.255-10.745 24-24 24H24c-13.255 0-24-10.745-24-24V200c0-13.255 10.745-24 24-24h48c13.255 0 24 10.745 24 24zM68 368c0-11.046-8.954-20-20-20s-20 8.954-20 20 8.954 20 20 20 20-8.954 20-20z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Send the Message:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Send this message to the number </span><b>105</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_ff9a0b-03"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_hand-point-right kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 512 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M512 199.652c0 23.625-20.65 43.826-44.8 43.826h-99.851c16.34 17.048 18.346 49.766-6.299 70.944 14.288 22.829 2.147 53.017-16.45 62.315C353.574 425.878 322.654 448 272 448c-2.746 0-13.276-.203-16-.195-61.971.168-76.894-31.065-123.731-38.315C120.596 407.683 112 397.599 112 385.786V214.261l.002-.001c.011-18.366 10.607-35.889 28.464-43.845 28.886-12.994 95.413-49.038 107.534-77.323 7.797-18.194 21.384-29.084 40-29.092 34.222-.014 57.752 35.098 44.119 66.908-3.583 8.359-8.312 16.67-14.153 24.918H467.2c23.45 0 44.8 20.543 44.8 43.826zM96 200v192c0 13.255-10.745 24-24 24H24c-13.255 0-24-10.745-24-24V200c0-13.255 10.745-24 24-24h48c13.255 0 24 10.745 24 24zM68 368c0-11.046-8.954-20-20-20s-20 8.954-20 20 8.954 20 20 20 20-8.954 20-20z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Receive the Verification</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">: Wait for a response from the service, which will provide you with the details of your National Identity Card.</span></span></li>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id11_b590d4-4b alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_6e7321-0b"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-60f9566d232c001086a9ad731c3b15e0">Botar NID Card Check</h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">BOTAR NID Card Check refers to the process of verifying National Identity Cards using the BOTAR (Biometric and Optical Recognition Technology for Accurate Records) system.</span></p>



<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items11_01de87-9e kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_59b504-dd"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Biometric Recognition: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">BOTAR uses biometric data such as fingerprints, facial recognition, and iris scans to verify the identity of the cardholder. This data is unique to each individual, making it highly reliable for identification purposes.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_f33136-68"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Optical Recognition: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">The system also employs optical recognition technology to check the physical features of the NID card. This includes scanning holograms, watermarks, and other security features embedded in the card.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_edda62-b3"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Database Cross-Referencing: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">Once the biometric and optical data are collected, BOTAR cross-references this information with national databases to confirm the authenticity of the NID card. This ensures that the card details match the records held by the issuing authority.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_605743-a0"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><b>Real-Time Verification: </b><span style="font-weight: 400;">BOTAR provides real-time verification, meaning that the authenticity of an NID card can be confirmed instantly. This is particularly useful in high-security areas or situations requiring immediate identity verification.</span></span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>

</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_e733cc-85"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-729a89f6a3ee800b7e31e22a479798d9">NID Card Check Offline</h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>Follow these steps to check NID card details and authenticity offline.</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items11_475a1d-f7 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_72fbb3-36"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_wifiOff kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="1" y1="1" x2="23" y2="23"/><path d="M16.72 11.06A10.94 10.94 0 0 1 19 12.55"/><path d="M5 12.55a10.94 10.94 0 0 1 5.17-2.39"/><path d="M10.71 5.05A16 16 0 0 1 22.58 9"/><path d="M1.42 9a15.91 15.91 0 0 1 4.7-2.88"/><path d="M8.53 16.11a6 6 0 0 1 6.95 0"/><line x1="12" y1="20" x2="12" y2="20"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Visit a Local Election Commission Office:</strong> Go to the nearest Election Commission office or a designated service centre where NID card services are provided.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_689614-8b"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_wifiOff kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="1" y1="1" x2="23" y2="23"/><path d="M16.72 11.06A10.94 10.94 0 0 1 19 12.55"/><path d="M5 12.55a10.94 10.94 0 0 1 5.17-2.39"/><path d="M10.71 5.05A16 16 0 0 1 22.58 9"/><path d="M1.42 9a15.91 15.91 0 0 1 4.7-2.88"/><path d="M8.53 16.11a6 6 0 0 1 6.95 0"/><line x1="12" y1="20" x2="12" y2="20"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Fill Out the Verification Form:</strong> Obtain and fill out the NID verification form available at the office. This form will require basic details such as the NID number, name, and other relevant information.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_0a30bd-44"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_wifiOff kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="1" y1="1" x2="23" y2="23"/><path d="M16.72 11.06A10.94 10.94 0 0 1 19 12.55"/><path d="M5 12.55a10.94 10.94 0 0 1 5.17-2.39"/><path d="M10.71 5.05A16 16 0 0 1 22.58 9"/><path d="M1.42 9a15.91 15.91 0 0 1 4.7-2.88"/><path d="M8.53 16.11a6 6 0 0 1 6.95 0"/><line x1="12" y1="20" x2="12" y2="20"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Submit Required Documents:</strong> Submit the filled-out verification form along with the necessary supporting documents. These documents may include a photocopy of the NID card, a passport-sized photograph, and any other identification documents as required by the office.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_c28544-46"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_wifiOff kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="1" y1="1" x2="23" y2="23"/><path d="M16.72 11.06A10.94 10.94 0 0 1 19 12.55"/><path d="M5 12.55a10.94 10.94 0 0 1 5.17-2.39"/><path d="M10.71 5.05A16 16 0 0 1 22.58 9"/><path d="M1.42 9a15.91 15.91 0 0 1 4.7-2.88"/><path d="M8.53 16.11a6 6 0 0 1 6.95 0"/><line x1="12" y1="20" x2="12" y2="20"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Provide Biometric Information:</strong> At the service center, you may need to provide biometric information such as fingerprints or a retina scan for verification purposes.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_e8c79c-30"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_wifiOff kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="1" y1="1" x2="23" y2="23"/><path d="M16.72 11.06A10.94 10.94 0 0 1 19 12.55"/><path d="M5 12.55a10.94 10.94 0 0 1 5.17-2.39"/><path d="M10.71 5.05A16 16 0 0 1 22.58 9"/><path d="M1.42 9a15.91 15.91 0 0 1 4.7-2.88"/><path d="M8.53 16.11a6 6 0 0 1 6.95 0"/><line x1="12" y1="20" x2="12" y2="20"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Pay the Processing Fee:</strong> Pay the required fee for the NID verification service. The fee amount will be specified by the Election Commission office.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_e60e58-46"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_wifiOff kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="1" y1="1" x2="23" y2="23"/><path d="M16.72 11.06A10.94 10.94 0 0 1 19 12.55"/><path d="M5 12.55a10.94 10.94 0 0 1 5.17-2.39"/><path d="M10.71 5.05A16 16 0 0 1 22.58 9"/><path d="M1.42 9a15.91 15.91 0 0 1 4.7-2.88"/><path d="M8.53 16.11a6 6 0 0 1 6.95 0"/><line x1="12" y1="20" x2="12" y2="20"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Receive Acknowledgment Receipt:</strong> After submitting the form and documents, you will receive an acknowledgment receipt. This receipt will have a reference number which you can use for follow-up.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_70193b-b8"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_wifiOff kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="1" y1="1" x2="23" y2="23"/><path d="M16.72 11.06A10.94 10.94 0 0 1 19 12.55"/><path d="M5 12.55a10.94 10.94 0 0 1 5.17-2.39"/><path d="M10.71 5.05A16 16 0 0 1 22.58 9"/><path d="M1.42 9a15.91 15.91 0 0 1 4.7-2.88"/><path d="M8.53 16.11a6 6 0 0 1 6.95 0"/><line x1="12" y1="20" x2="12" y2="20"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Verification Process:</strong> The Election Commission office will process your request and verify the provided information against their database.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_a20276-da"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_wifiOff kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="1" y1="1" x2="23" y2="23"/><path d="M16.72 11.06A10.94 10.94 0 0 1 19 12.55"/><path d="M5 12.55a10.94 10.94 0 0 1 5.17-2.39"/><path d="M10.71 5.05A16 16 0 0 1 22.58 9"/><path d="M1.42 9a15.91 15.91 0 0 1 4.7-2.88"/><path d="M8.53 16.11a6 6 0 0 1 6.95 0"/><line x1="12" y1="20" x2="12" y2="20"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Collect Verification Result:</strong> Once the verification process is complete, visit the Election Commission office again with your acknowledgment receipt to collect the verification result. This result will confirm the authenticity of the NID card.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_e3bafe-74"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_wifiOff kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><line x1="1" y1="1" x2="23" y2="23"/><path d="M16.72 11.06A10.94 10.94 0 0 1 19 12.55"/><path d="M5 12.55a10.94 10.94 0 0 1 5.17-2.39"/><path d="M10.71 5.05A16 16 0 0 1 22.58 9"/><path d="M1.42 9a15.91 15.91 0 0 1 4.7-2.88"/><path d="M8.53 16.11a6 6 0 0 1 6.95 0"/><line x1="12" y1="20" x2="12" y2="20"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Follow Up if Necessary:</strong> If there are any discrepancies or additional information required, the office will notify you. Follow up with the necessary details to complete the verification process.</span></li>
</ul></div>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_a26257-03"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-06116d73e4f1bb25af8605f27878c47a">Check Old NID Card Online</h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>Check Old NID Card Online in Bangladeshis very easy and simple to follow these steps:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items11_b15e7b-80 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_76d337-9e"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Visit the NID Service Website: </strong>To start, go to the official NID services website: <a href="https://services.nidw.gov.bd/nid-pub/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://services.nidw.gov.bd/nid-pub/</a>.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_5a0e3d-e2"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Register for an Account: </strong>On the homepage, click on the &#8220;<strong>Register</strong>&#8221; button to create a new account. If you already have an account, you can log in with your credentials.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_b4d6d7-f5"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Enter Required Information: </strong>You will be asked to enter your &#8220;<strong>National Identity Card Number</strong>&#8221; and &#8220;<strong>Date of Birth</strong>&#8220;. After providing this information, click on the &#8220;<strong>Submit</strong>&#8221; button to proceed.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_854f1f-a0"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Verify Your Address: </strong>Once you submit the required details, you will be prompted to verify your &#8220;<strong>Current and Permanent Addresses</strong>&#8220;. This is done to ensure that the details match the records available with the authorities.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_b9cefd-b7"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Access Your Information:</strong> After completing the verification process, you will be able to access and view the details of your old &#8220;<strong>NID Card Online</strong>&#8220;. You can also make updates if necessary, depending on the type of changes required.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_bb43c5-2b"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Download or Print:</strong> If needed, you can download or print your NID details for future use, including verification purposes.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id11_ab9a06-3f alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_4bed63-82"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-f61ef37d57abbf096d3213ad04a6a01c">Other Methods to Check the National Identity Card</h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Method 01</h3>



<p>The official way to verify anyone&#8217;s National Identity Card (NID) information is to go to the Upazila Election Commission Office or the NID Wing at the main Election Commission Office in Agargaon, Dhaka. You can verify the NID and collect a verified copy for a fee.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Method 02</h3>



<p>Land Development Tax (LDTax) website provides detailed NID information, including name and photograph. Users could view the person&#8217;s name, photo, and address by entering their NID number and mobile number.</p>



<p>Recent database security reasons have led to the Election Commission disabling this option. LDTax allows you to verify your NID number. Register an account at ldtax.gov.bd by providing your mobile number and password, and then go to your profile to verify your NID.</p>



<p>Using your NID number and date of birth, you can verify your NID information. It is used to pay land development taxes, but it can also verify voter ID cards by creating a single account. If an NID has already been used to create an account, it cannot be used again.</p>



<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-infobox kt-info-box11_3626ac-f6"><span class="kt-blocks-info-box-link-wrap info-box-link kt-blocks-info-box-media-align-top kt-info-halign-center"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media-container"><div class="kt-blocks-info-box-media kt-info-media-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-image-inner-intrisic-container"><div class="kadence-info-box-image-intrisic kt-info-animate-none"><div class="kadence-info-box-image-inner-intrisic"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" src="https://nidcardonlinechecks.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/Capture-14.png" alt="" width="288" height="296" class="kt-info-box-image wp-image-49"/></div></div></div></div></div><div class="kt-infobox-textcontent"><h2 class="kt-blocks-info-box-title"><b>What is a NID Card?</b></h2><p class="kt-blocks-info-box-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The National Identity Card (NID) is a mandatory identification document issued to every Bangladeshi citizen by the Bangladesh Election Commission upon reaching the age of 18. The NID card is a biometric, smart identity card embedded with a microchip.</span></p></div></span></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id11_95b08c-8b alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_19d22a-6f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-e9f111f12d22622f022bb88fc5e653e8"><b><strong>What is NID Number?</strong></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The NID number refers to the unique identification number assigned to citizens in Bangladesh. It can be found on either the 17-digit national identity (NID) card or the 10-digit smart national identity card (SNID).</span></p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id11_e2d890-e1 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_5bbf9b-6f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-2af4b2400bcbf05d689b64daf771355b"><strong>Who Can Use NID Card?</strong></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>It is a compulsory identity document issued to every Bangladeshi citizen upon reaching the age of 18 by the Bangladesh Election Commission (EC). Here is a step-by-step breakdown of who can use the NID card.</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items11_5bc66b-93 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_e663b8-42"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Bangladeshi Citizens Aged 18 and Above:</strong> Every citizen who has reached the age of 18 is eligible to receive and use the NID card.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_3c124c-1a"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Government Agencies:</strong> Various government bodies use the NID card for verifying the identity of citizens during the provision of public services.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_05a56c-e2"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Financial Institutions:</strong> Banks and other financial institutions use the NID card for identity verification to open accounts, process loans, and other financial transactions.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_37ebd4-30"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Educational Institutions:</strong> Schools, colleges, and universities may use the NID card to verify the identity of students during admissions and examinations.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_71ed56-ec"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Healthcare Services:</strong> Hospitals and clinics use the NID card to confirm the identity of patients and maintain accurate medical records.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_309226-4b"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Telecommunication Companies:</strong> Telecom providers require the NID card for issuing SIM cards and verifying the identity of their customers.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_07b265-27"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Employment Verification: </strong>Employers use the NID card to verify the identity of potential and current employees.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_85d0c4-95"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Voting :</strong>The NID card is used by citizens to identify themselves at polling stations during elections.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_0aef4f-92"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Travel and Transportation:</strong> The NID card can be used as an identification document for domestic travel and for some services provided by transportation companies.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_20be69-3e"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Property Transactions:</strong> The NID card is used to verify the identity of individuals involved in buying, selling, or renting property.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id11_d6421f-40 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_25b481-0d"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-d574cd8e628cdcdfa9a49542456d84bc"><strong>Who is Eligible for NID Card?</strong></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>To be eligible for a National Identity (NID) Card in Bangladesh, individuals must meet the following criteria:</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items11_e2c487-a5 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_df4419-a5"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Citizenship:</strong> Must be a Bangladeshi citizen.</span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_1258d5-16"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Age Requirement:</strong> Must be at least 18 years of age.</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id11_c6774a-d8 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_f892c3-1e"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-cdf57a53fa4700fb8eadd3610f0184cb"><b>Required Documents for NID Card Registration</b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-image kb-image11_0c548b-b3"><figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="600" height="700" src="https://nidcardonlinechecks.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/SSC-or-equivalent-certificate-Birth-certificate-Passport-driving-licence-or-TIN-certificate-if-available-Utility-bill-copy-house-rent-receipt-or-holding-tax-receipt-as-proof-of-address-.png" alt="" class="kb-img wp-image-900" srcset="https://nidcardonlinechecks.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/SSC-or-equivalent-certificate-Birth-certificate-Passport-driving-licence-or-TIN-certificate-if-available-Utility-bill-copy-house-rent-receipt-or-holding-tax-receipt-as-proof-of-address-.png 600w, https://nidcardonlinechecks.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/SSC-or-equivalent-certificate-Birth-certificate-Passport-driving-licence-or-TIN-certificate-if-available-Utility-bill-copy-house-rent-receipt-or-holding-tax-receipt-as-proof-of-address--257x300.png 257w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px" /></figure></div>



<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">To apply for a National Identity Card (NID), you will need to provide the following documents:</span></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items11_98f18b-25 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_2bcc97-15"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_file-export kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 576 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M384 121.9c0-6.3-2.5-12.4-7-16.9L279.1 7c-4.5-4.5-10.6-7-17-7H256v128h128v-6.1zM192 336v-32c0-8.84 7.16-16 16-16h176V160H248c-13.2 0-24-10.8-24-24V0H24C10.7 0 0 10.7 0 24v464c0 13.3 10.7 24 24 24h336c13.3 0 24-10.7 24-24V352H208c-8.84 0-16-7.16-16-16zm379.05-28.02l-95.7-96.43c-10.06-10.14-27.36-3.01-27.36 11.27V288H384v64h63.99v65.18c0 14.28 17.29 21.41 27.36 11.27l95.7-96.42c6.6-6.66 6.6-17.4 0-24.05z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">SSC or equivalent certificate</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_664c11-5e"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_file-export kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 576 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M384 121.9c0-6.3-2.5-12.4-7-16.9L279.1 7c-4.5-4.5-10.6-7-17-7H256v128h128v-6.1zM192 336v-32c0-8.84 7.16-16 16-16h176V160H248c-13.2 0-24-10.8-24-24V0H24C10.7 0 0 10.7 0 24v464c0 13.3 10.7 24 24 24h336c13.3 0 24-10.7 24-24V352H208c-8.84 0-16-7.16-16-16zm379.05-28.02l-95.7-96.43c-10.06-10.14-27.36-3.01-27.36 11.27V288H384v64h63.99v65.18c0 14.28 17.29 21.41 27.36 11.27l95.7-96.42c6.6-6.66 6.6-17.4 0-24.05z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;"><a href="https://birthcertificatechecksbd.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Birth certificate</a></span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_11d9ba-8d"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_file-export kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 576 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M384 121.9c0-6.3-2.5-12.4-7-16.9L279.1 7c-4.5-4.5-10.6-7-17-7H256v128h128v-6.1zM192 336v-32c0-8.84 7.16-16 16-16h176V160H248c-13.2 0-24-10.8-24-24V0H24C10.7 0 0 10.7 0 24v464c0 13.3 10.7 24 24 24h336c13.3 0 24-10.7 24-24V352H208c-8.84 0-16-7.16-16-16zm379.05-28.02l-95.7-96.43c-10.06-10.14-27.36-3.01-27.36 11.27V288H384v64h63.99v65.18c0 14.28 17.29 21.41 27.36 11.27l95.7-96.42c6.6-6.66 6.6-17.4 0-24.05z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Passport, <a href="https://brtaserviceportal.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">driving licence</a>, or TIN certificate (if available)</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_91fae8-f9"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_file-export kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 576 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M384 121.9c0-6.3-2.5-12.4-7-16.9L279.1 7c-4.5-4.5-10.6-7-17-7H256v128h128v-6.1zM192 336v-32c0-8.84 7.16-16 16-16h176V160H248c-13.2 0-24-10.8-24-24V0H24C10.7 0 0 10.7 0 24v464c0 13.3 10.7 24 24 24h336c13.3 0 24-10.7 24-24V352H208c-8.84 0-16-7.16-16-16zm379.05-28.02l-95.7-96.43c-10.06-10.14-27.36-3.01-27.36 11.27V288H384v64h63.99v65.18c0 14.28 17.29 21.41 27.36 11.27l95.7-96.42c6.6-6.66 6.6-17.4 0-24.05z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Utility bill copy, house rent receipt, or holding tax receipt (as proof of address)</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_72bd7f-58"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_file-export kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 576 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M384 121.9c0-6.3-2.5-12.4-7-16.9L279.1 7c-4.5-4.5-10.6-7-17-7H256v128h128v-6.1zM192 336v-32c0-8.84 7.16-16 16-16h176V160H248c-13.2 0-24-10.8-24-24V0H24C10.7 0 0 10.7 0 24v464c0 13.3 10.7 24 24 24h336c13.3 0 24-10.7 24-24V352H208c-8.84 0-16-7.16-16-16zm379.05-28.02l-95.7-96.43c-10.06-10.14-27.36-3.01-27.36 11.27V288H384v64h63.99v65.18c0 14.28 17.29 21.41 27.36 11.27l95.7-96.42c6.6-6.66 6.6-17.4 0-24.05z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Citizenship certificate (if applicable)</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_68e197-88"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_file-export kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 576 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M384 121.9c0-6.3-2.5-12.4-7-16.9L279.1 7c-4.5-4.5-10.6-7-17-7H256v128h128v-6.1zM192 336v-32c0-8.84 7.16-16 16-16h176V160H248c-13.2 0-24-10.8-24-24V0H24C10.7 0 0 10.7 0 24v464c0 13.3 10.7 24 24 24h336c13.3 0 24-10.7 24-24V352H208c-8.84 0-16-7.16-16-16zm379.05-28.02l-95.7-96.43c-10.06-10.14-27.36-3.01-27.36 11.27V288H384v64h63.99v65.18c0 14.28 17.29 21.41 27.36 11.27l95.7-96.42c6.6-6.66 6.6-17.4 0-24.05z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Attested photocopy of the NID of father, mother, husband, or wife</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_b7d6c6-d7"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_file-export kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 576 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M384 121.9c0-6.3-2.5-12.4-7-16.9L279.1 7c-4.5-4.5-10.6-7-17-7H256v128h128v-6.1zM192 336v-32c0-8.84 7.16-16 16-16h176V160H248c-13.2 0-24-10.8-24-24V0H24C10.7 0 0 10.7 0 24v464c0 13.3 10.7 24 24 24h336c13.3 0 24-10.7 24-24V352H208c-8.84 0-16-7.16-16-16zm379.05-28.02l-95.7-96.43c-10.06-10.14-27.36-3.01-27.36 11.27V288H384v64h63.99v65.18c0 14.28 17.29 21.41 27.36 11.27l95.7-96.42c6.6-6.66 6.6-17.4 0-24.05z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">You must be physically present at the Election Commission (EC) premises for photo and biometric data collection.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_7c9541-2f"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_file-export kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 576 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M384 121.9c0-6.3-2.5-12.4-7-16.9L279.1 7c-4.5-4.5-10.6-7-17-7H256v128h128v-6.1zM192 336v-32c0-8.84 7.16-16 16-16h176V160H248c-13.2 0-24-10.8-24-24V0H24C10.7 0 0 10.7 0 24v464c0 13.3 10.7 24 24 24h336c13.3 0 24-10.7 24-24V352H208c-8.84 0-16-7.16-16-16zm379.05-28.02l-95.7-96.43c-10.06-10.14-27.36-3.01-27.36 11.27V288H384v64h63.99v65.18c0 14.28 17.29 21.41 27.36 11.27l95.7-96.42c6.6-6.66 6.6-17.4 0-24.05z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><a href="https://medicalreportcheckbd.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Medical Report</a> (Optional)</span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id11_a412ec-ba alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_aed12d-7e"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-ba4183550c828226751af15e491e89a7"><strong>NID Card Online Registration</strong></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">To initiate the NID Card Registration process, you have two options:</span></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id11_e9ca1d-d1 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_d03533-18"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b> Apply Online</b></h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items11_54eaf5-6f kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_e7a78c-89"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Visit the NID Application System.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_696d69-1a"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Register an account using your Name and date of Birth.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_9695d3-17"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Create a username and password.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_75b336-46"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Input your personal details and address.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_3a96e0-4f"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Submit the printed copy of the Application form along with required documents to the election office.</span></span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id11_2f95df-8b alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_d87627-31"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><b><strong> Submit a Voter Registration Form in Person</strong></b></b></h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items11_189199-4e kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_9a38ea-8b"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Visit the Election office.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_e4e1cf-e2"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Fill out a Voter Registration form.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_5fbbad-b6"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Provide necessary documents.</span></span></li>
</ul></div>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id11_98e204-94 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_c232ce-06"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-8deb09fac505a10da88f1f9fff6d1b9f"><b><strong>How to Check NID Real or Fake?</strong></b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Here are the steps to check if an NID (National Identity Card) is real or fake:</span></p>



<p></p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id11_6d016a-f0 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_49763b-0f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><strong><b>Check NID Real or Fake</b> <b>Via SMS</b></strong></h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items11_500e0e-5d kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_bf4d78-37"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Type NID &lt;Space&gt; Form Number &lt;Space&gt; <strong>Date of Birth</strong> as <strong>DD-MM-YY</strong>.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_81ed1d-c1"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Send the SMS to<strong> 105</strong>.</span></span></li>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_12e4e3-06"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><b><strong>Check NID Real or Fake</strong> Via<b> Online Verification</b></b></h3>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-iconlist kt-svg-icon-list-items kt-svg-icon-list-items11_2aab69-38 kt-svg-icon-list-columns-1 alignnone"><ul class="kt-svg-icon-list">
<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_733249-26"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Visit the official website: </span><a href="https://services.nidw.gov.bd/nid-pub/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">https://services.nidw.gov.bd/nid-pub/</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_0f798c-23"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Create an account if you don&#8217;t have one.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_03300a-ab"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Log in to your account.</span></span></li>



<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_1703a2-2f"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fe_checkCircle kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"  fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Check your NID card by providing the necessary details.</span></span></li>
</ul></div>



<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Once your application is verified, you will be contacted to have your photograph and fingerprints taken, and you will receive a slip for the voter registration form. If your application is approved, you can download your new voter ID card online within 10-15 days of providing biometrics.</span></p>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id11_4701f0-d9 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_9c5562-5c"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-afbc218642024eac6e8e8da040152e35"><strong>Benefits of NID Card</strong></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>Benefits of NID Card extend to various aspects of citizens&#8217; rights and ease of use:</p>



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-border-color" style="border-color:#4e6c50"><tbody><tr><td><strong>Citizens&#8217; Rights and Benefits</strong></td><td>It serves as a fundamental document for asserting citizenship rights and accessing government-provided benefits and services.</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Driving License</strong></td><td>Required as a primary identification document for obtaining a driving license, ensuring safer road practices.</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Passport</strong></td><td>Essential for passport application and travel documentation, facilitating international travel and mobility.</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Property Transactions</strong></td><td>Necessary for buying and selling property, ensuring legal and transparent land transactions.</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Opening Bangladeshi Bank Accounts</strong></td><td>Vital for opening bank accounts in Bangladesh, enabling financial inclusion and access to banking services.</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Account Verification</strong></td><td>Used for verifying accounts, ensuring security and authenticity in financial transactions.</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Bank Loan Support</strong></td><td>Often required as proof of identity and citizenship when applying for bank loans, facilitating access to financial support.</td></tr><tr><td><strong>Government Pensions</strong></td><td>Required for availing government pension schemes, ensuring retirees receive their entitled benefits.</td></tr></tbody></table></figure>



<p></p>

<li class="wp-block-kadence-listitem kt-svg-icon-list-item-wrap kt-svg-icon-list-item-11_e41155-02"><span class="kb-svg-icon-wrap kb-svg-icon-fas_address-card kt-svg-icon-list-single"><svg viewBox="0 0 576 512"  fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  aria-hidden="true"><path d="M528 32H48C21.5 32 0 53.5 0 80v352c0 26.5 21.5 48 48 48h480c26.5 0 48-21.5 48-48V80c0-26.5-21.5-48-48-48zm-352 96c35.3 0 64 28.7 64 64s-28.7 64-64 64-64-28.7-64-64 28.7-64 64-64zm112 236.8c0 10.6-10 19.2-22.4 19.2H86.4C74 384 64 375.4 64 364.8v-19.2c0-31.8 30.1-57.6 67.2-57.6h5c12.3 5.1 25.7 8 39.8 8s27.6-2.9 39.8-8h5c37.1 0 67.2 25.8 67.2 57.6v19.2zM512 312c0 4.4-3.6 8-8 8H360c-4.4 0-8-3.6-8-8v-16c0-4.4 3.6-8 8-8h144c4.4 0 8 3.6 8 8v16zm0-64c0 4.4-3.6 8-8 8H360c-4.4 0-8-3.6-8-8v-16c0-4.4 3.6-8 8-8h144c4.4 0 8 3.6 8 8v16zm0-64c0 4.4-3.6 8-8 8H360c-4.4 0-8-3.6-8-8v-16c0-4.4 3.6-8 8-8h144c4.4 0 8 3.6 8 8v16z"/></svg></span><span class="kt-svg-icon-list-text"><strong>Cost-Effective:</strong> Utilizing NID Card Check can be cost-effective for organizations compared to traditional methods of identity verification, as it reduces paperwork and manual processing efforts.</span></li>
</ul></div>
