<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id11_7829b2-24 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_9f1e40-62"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-0ce39afc0d4995bfe0b16c5944bd2ef0"><b>FAQs About NID Card Check</b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-accordion alignnone"><div class="kt-accordion-wrap kt-accordion-id11_b0c15f-e8 kt-accordion-has-10-panes kt-active-pane-0 kt-accordion-block kt-pane-header-alignment-left kt-accodion-icon-style-basic kt-accodion-icon-side-right" style="max-width:none"><div class="kt-accordion-inner-wrap" data-allow-multiple-open="false" data-start-open="0">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-4 kt-pane11_7cde41-4e"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">How to get voter ID card?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Rules for extracting an online copy <strong>of NID card</strong></p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Go to the website <a href="http://services.nidw.gov.bd" target="_blank" rel="noopener">services.nidw.gov.bd</a></li>



<li>Please check the slip number/ national identity card number and date of birth.</li>



<li>Save the current and permanent address.</li>



<li>Verify your mobile number.</li>



<li>NID wallet face verification.</li>



<li>Download an online copy of the <strong>NID profile.</strong></li>
</ul>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-1 kt-pane11_7e84fa-62"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><b>What is a smart nid card?</b></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">A NID is also a biometric, microchip-embedded smart identity card. Bangladeshi citizens are required to have an NID for a variety of public and private services.</span></p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-2 kt-pane11_2b9d33-17"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><b>How to know nid number by SMS?</b></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The simplest way to check your NID or Voter ID card is to send an SMS from your mobile phone. Type NID &lt;Space&gt; Form Number &lt;Space&gt; Date of Birth as DD-MM-YY and send it to 105. You can check your NID card online by visiting https://services.nidw.gov.bd/nid-pub/.</span></p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-3 kt-pane11_d8570f-db"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><b>What is NID used for?</b></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">It is a device that serves as the demarcation point between the carrier&#8217;s local loop and the customer&#8217;s premises wiring in telecommunications.</span></p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-5 kt-pane11_2f671c-98"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How can I check my smart card status by SMS?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>You can get information about the generation by sending NP space DRC to 26969. You can check your smart card status by visiting this link- <a href="https://services.nidw.gov.bd/nidpub/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://services.nidw.gov.bd/nidpub/</a>card-status.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-6 kt-pane11_fea37f-70"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How to check if NID card is ready?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>Visit the Official Website:</strong> Check the official portal of the NID issuing authority.</li>



<li><strong>Log into the NID Portal: </strong>Use your registration or NID number to log in and check the status.</li>



<li><strong>Use SMS Services: </strong>Send a text with your NID or reference number to the designated number.</li>



<li><strong>Check via Mobile App:</strong> Use the official app provided by the NID authority (if available).</li>



<li><strong>Visit the NID Office: </strong>Go to the local NID office in person with your application details.</li>



<li><strong>Call the Helpline:</strong> Contact the official NID helpline or customer support for assistance.</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-7 kt-pane11_2cf8c1-b9"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How to check voter ID card?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>On the Election Commission&#8217;s website, a service called Voter Information previously checked voter ID cards, but it has since been closed.<br>Voter information can only be verified via SMS.<br>You can also check the accuracy of voter ID card information by going to an election office or other government department that offers service through NID.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-8 kt-pane11_9f9b5e-f3"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How to Check the Delivery Status of Your NID Card in Bangladesh</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>To check the delivery status of your NID card in Bangladesh, visit the official Election Commission website, enter your NID number or application details, and track the progress. Alternatively, you can use the NID service portal or contact local NID offices for updates on delivery status.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-9 kt-pane11_39191f-1a"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How to get a smart card?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>After registering as a new voter, some people do not receive smart cards for a long time. Smart cards are difficult to print, which is the main reason. If your smart card is printed, you will receive it through the smart card distribution program. The good news is that people can get a smart card for free once, and getting one again the second time, i.e. if they lose it, is a hassle and expense.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-10 kt-pane11_12b95b-18"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What is required to check the voter ID card?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>You must provide your national identification card number/form number, date of birth, address, mobile number, and face verification to check your voter ID card.</p>
</div></div></div>
</div></div></div>



<p></p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-1ad6dce22334b882327d205d084b8de3"><b>Conclusion&nbsp;</b></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p></p>



<p>The NID Card Check service is an essential tool for verifying citizens&#8217; identities, offering convenience and reliability for various purposes in Bangladesh. Whether accessed online or offline, this service aids in preventing fraud, ensuring accurate identification, and facilitating access to essential services across different sectors.</p>
